<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:запеть.html>запо́й</a> (12106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запить.html>запи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запеть.html>запо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запой.html>запо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запой.html>запо́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запой.html>запо́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>binge, bout, drinking bout (recurring drunkenness due to a pathological craving for alcoholic drink; a period of continuous drunkenness)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недельный.html>неде́льный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запеть.html>запо́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nedélʹnyj <b>zapój</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">week-long binge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:частый.html>ча́стые</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запой.html>запо́и</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">částyje <b>zapói</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">frequent binges</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>booze</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> binge (without stopping, in immoderate quantities; with unbridled enthusiasm)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запеть.html>запо́ем</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kurítʹ <b>zapójem</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">have a smoking binge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:запеть.html>запо́ем</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čitátʹ <b>zapójem</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">have a reading binge</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запеть.html>запо́ем</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapójem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запойный.html>запо́йный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapójnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***заполонить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заполонить.html>заполони́ть</a> (24498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">полони́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заполонить.html>заполони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zapolonítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заполоня́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take prisoner, to take captive</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to captivate, to charm</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fill up (a space, a place)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">take captive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пленить.html>плени́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">plenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
